Newsreader 16pt Regular (Newsreader[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '

NID 6 is 'Newsreader16pt-Regular', Everything looks good.

Newsreader 16pt Regular (Newsreader[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16

Name table entry according Monotype

NID 16 and 17 is not required for a variable font. In case you have good reasons, please keep it, otherwise please remove it.

Warning

Newsreader 16pt Regular (Newsreader[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

If NID 2 and 17 = 'Regular': MS NID 16 should match NID 1.
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). This is true for MS Office Version 1639 and lower. Even though Microsoft has changed it with version 1640 (fast insider, June 2020) we keep this as an error, because most of the current MS Office users won't update in the near future. More infos here:
Cross Platform Issues

NID 16 and 17 is not required for a variable font. In case you have good reasons, please keep it, otherwise please remove it.
(NID 16) 'Newsreader' ≠ 'Newsreader 16pt' (NID 1).

Pass

Newsreader 16pt Italic (Newsreader-Italic[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Newsreader16pt-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

MS NID 8 is 'Production Type', but should be one of these: 'Monotype Imaging Inc.', 'Monotype Imaging Inc', 'Monotype ITC Inc.', 'Monotype Hong Kong Limited', 'Monotype Limited', 'Monotype KK', 'Monotype Solutions India Private Limited', 'Monotype GmbH', 'MyFonts Inc.', 'MyFonts Inc', 'Fontsmith Ltd.', 'Fontsmith Ltd'.

Error

Newsreader 16pt Italic (Newsreader-Italic[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

NID 11 is http://www.productiontype.com/, but should be http://www.monotype.com. Please verify against job spec.

License text

MS NID 13 is:
This Font Software is licensed under the SIL Open Font License, Version 1.1. This license is available with a FAQ at: http://scripts.sil.org/OFL
, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

MS NID 16

Name table entry according Monotype

Warning

Newsreader 16pt Italic (Newsreader-Italic[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 and 17 is not required for a variable font. In case you have good reasons, please keep it, otherwise please remove it.
(NID 16 + 'Space' + NID 17) 'Newsreader Italic' ≠ 'Newsreader 16pt Italic' (NID 1 + 'Space' + NID 2).

Pass
